\DoxyCodeLine{   :: \textcolor{stringliteral}{"r0"});\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{/*lint -\/restore Enable MISRA rule (2.1,1.1) checking. */}\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{   if (++SR\_lock == 1u) \{\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     SR\_reg = SR\_reg\_local;\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{   \}\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{ \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(0)}
